1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
```

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# ArangoDB Authentication and Authorization Audit

## Your Task

Audit the authentication and authorization infrastructure in ArangoDB. Find all C++ source files in `arangodb/arangodb` that implement auth: 1. The file under `arangod/Auth/` or `arangod/RestHandler/` that implements user authentication (look for `AuthenticationHandler` or `UserManager`). 2. The file that implements JWT token validation for the REST API. 3. The file that defines `ExecContext` or the authorization context that checks permissions for database operations. 4. The file under `arangod/RestHandler/` that implements the `/_api/user` REST endpoint for user management. 5. The configuration file or source that defines default authentication settings (`arangosh` or `arangod` startup options). Report each file path and key class/function.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/arangodb--a5cca0b8` (arangodb/arangodb)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive audit of the ArangoDB authentication and authorization infrastructure. The findings have been written to `/workspace/answer.json`.

## Summary of Findings

The audit identified the complete authentication and authorization infrastructure across 18 C++ source/header files:

### Key Components Found:

1. **User Authentication Handler** (`RestAuthHandler`): Handles REST API authentication requests and JWT generation via `/_open/auth` endpoint

2. **JWT Token Validation** (`TokenCache`): Validates both basic auth and JWT tokens, supporting HMAC-SHA256 and ES256 (ECDSA) signature algorithms

3. **Authorization Context** (`ExecContext`): Maintains execution context with user permissions, providing methods to check superuser status, admin rights, and database/collection access levels

4. **User Management REST API** (`RestUsersHandler`): Implements `/_api/user/` endpoint for creating, reading, updating, and deleting users

5. **User Manager** (`UserManager`/`UserManagerImpl`): Central authority for user data, permissions caching, and background synchronization from `_system/_users` collection

6. **Authentication Feature** (`AuthenticationFeature`): Manages authentication initialization and configuration with startup options

7. **Configuration Defaults** (`AuthenticationOptions`): Defines default auth settings including 1-hour session timeout, 10-3600 second JWT expiry window

8. **Auth Handler Interface** (`Handler`): Pluggable interface for authentication handlers

9. **Permission Levels** (`auth::Level` enum): NONE, RO (read-only), RW (read-write) permission model

The audit includes detailed documentation of the authentication flow, security features, and all relevant symbol locations in the answer.json file.

\"## ArangoDB Authentication and Authorization Infrastructure Audit\\n\\nThe authentication and authorization infrastructure in ArangoDB is implemented across multiple components:\\n\\n### 1. Authentication Handler (User Authentication)\\n**Location:** `arangod/RestHandler/RestAuthHandler.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `RestAuthHandler` (inherits from `RestVocbaseBaseHandler`)\\n- **Responsibility:** Handles REST API authentication requests\\n- **Key Methods:**\\n  - `execute()`: Processes authentication requests\\n  - `generateJwt()`: Generates JWT tokens for authenticated users\\n- **Integration:** Registered at `/_open/auth` endpoint in `arangod/GeneralServer/GeneralServerFeature.cpp`\\n\\n### 2. JWT Token Validation\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/TokenCache.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `TokenCache`\\n- **Responsibility:** Caches and validates authentication tokens (both basic auth and JWT)\\n- **Key Methods:**\\n  - `checkAuthentication()`: Validates incoming auth tokens\\n  - `validateJwtBody()`: Parses and validates JWT token payload\\n  - `validateJwtHMAC256Signature()`: Validates HMAC-SHA256 JWT signatures\\n  - `validateJwtES256Signature()`: Validates ES256 (ECDSA) JWT signatures\\n- **Entry Structure:** Contains username, authentication status, expiry time, allowed paths, and roles\\n- **Features:**\\n  - Supports both HMAC-SHA256 and ES256 signature algorithms\\n  - Implements LRU cache for token entries\\n  - Manages both active and passive JWT secrets\\n\\n### 3. Authorization Context (Permission Checking)\\n**Location:** `arangod/Utils/ExecContext.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `ExecContext` (inherits from `RequestContext`)\\n- **Responsibility:** Maintains execution context with authorization information for each request\\n- **Key Features:**\\n  - Tracks current user, database, system-level auth level, and database-level auth level\\n  - Provides static `current()` method to access thread-local context\\n  - Implements superuser context via `ExecContext::Superuser` singleton\\n  - Methods:\\n    - `isSuperuser()`: Checks if user is superuser\\n    - `isAdminUser()`: Checks if user has admin privileges\\n    - `isInternal()`: Checks if context is internal operation\\n    - `isReadOnly()`: Checks if context is read-only\\n  - Uses scope guards: `ExecContextScope` and `ExecContextSuperuserScope`\\n\\n### 4. User Management REST API\\n**Location:** `arangod/RestHandler/RestUsersHandler.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `RestUsersHandler` (inherits from `RestBaseHandler`)\\n- **Responsibility:** Implements REST endpoint for user management\\n- **Endpoint:** `/_api/user/` (registered in `GeneralServerFeature`)\\n- **Supported Methods:**\\n  - `getRequest()`: List or retrieve user information\\n  - `postRequest()`: Create new user\\n  - `putRequest()`: Update user\\n  - `patchRequest()`: Partially update user\\n  - `deleteRequest()`: Delete user\\n- **Integration:** Uses `auth::UserManager` for persistence and `ExecContext` for authorization\\n\\n### 5. User Manager (User Data Management)\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/UserManager.h` (abstract interface) and `arangod/Auth/UserManagerImpl.h/cpp` (implementation)\\n- **Interface:** `UserManager` abstract base class\\n- **Implementation:** `UserManagerImpl` concrete class\\n- **Responsibility:** Central authority for user data, permissions, and caching\\n- **Key Features:**\\n  - Caches user data locally from `_system/_users` collection\\n  - Maintains background update thread for cache synchronization\\n  - Methods:\\n    - `storeUser()`: Create or replace user\\n    - `removeUser()`: Delete user\\n    - `updateUser()`: Update specific user\\n    - `accessUser()`: Read user without modification\\n    - `databaseAuthLevel()`: Check user's database permission\\n    - `collectionAuthLevel()`: Check user's collection permission\\n    - `checkCredentials()`: Validate username/password\\n    - `createAccessToken()`: Generate access tokens\\n    - `deleteAccessToken()`: Revoke access tokens\\n  - Thread-safe with read-write locks\\n\\n### 6. User Class\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/User.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `User`\\n- **Responsibility:** Represents a user object with permissions and metadata\\n- **Components:**\\n  - Username and password hash\\n  - Active/inactive status\\n  - Database-level permissions\\n  - Collection-level permissions\\n  - Extras (arbitrary metadata)\\n\\n### 7. Authentication Feature (Configuration)\\n**Location:** `arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `AuthenticationFeature`\\n- **Responsibility:** Manages authentication system initialization and configuration\\n- **Key Responsibilities:**\\n  - Collects command-line options via `collectOptions()` (registered in startup)\\n  - Validates options via `validateOptions()`\\n  - Initializes `UserManager` and `TokenCache` in `prepare()`\\n  - Loads JWT secrets from file/folder\\n  - Provides singleton access via `instance()` static method\\n  - Methods:\\n    - `isActive()`: Check if authentication is enabled\\n    - `authenticationUnixSockets()`: Check Unix socket auth setting\\n    - `authenticationSystemOnly()`: Check if auth restricted to system database\\n    - `tokenCache()`: Access token cache instance\\n    - `userManager()`: Access user manager instance\\n    - `jwtSecrets()`: Retrieve JWT secrets for token validation\\n    - `loadJwtSecretsFromFile()`: Load secrets from disk\\n\\n### 8. Authentication Options (Default Settings)\\n**Location:** `arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationOptions.h`\\n- **Structure:** `AuthenticationOptions`\\n- **Default Values:**\\n  - `authenticationUnixSockets = true`: Allow Unix socket auth\\n  - `authenticationSystemOnly = true`: Restrict to system database\\n  - `active = true`: Authentication enabled by default\\n  - `sessionTimeout = 3600.0` seconds: 1 hour default session timeout\\n  - `minimalJwtExpiryTime = 10.0` seconds: Minimum JWT expiry\\n  - `maximalJwtExpiryTime = 3600.0` seconds: Maximum JWT expiry (1 hour)\\n  - `jwtSecretProgramOption`: Optional inline JWT secret\\n  - `jwtSecretKeyfileProgramOption`: Optional JWT secret keyfile path\\n  - `jwtSecretFolderProgramOption`: Optional JWT secrets folder path\\n\\n### 9. Auth Handler Interface\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/Handler.h`\\n- **Class:** `Handler` abstract interface\\n- **Responsibility:** Defines interface for pluggable authentication handlers\\n- **Methods:**\\n  - `authenticate()`: Authenticate user and return permissions\\n  - `readPermissions()`: Read user permissions for cached users\\n  - `refreshRate()`: Return cache refresh rate in seconds\\n  - `allowOfflineCacheUsage()`: Allow use of offline cache\\n\\n### 10. Common Auth Definitions\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/Common.h`\\n- **Enum:** `Level` defines authorization levels:\\n  - `UNDEFINED (0)`: No level defined\\n  - `NONE (1)`: No access\\n  - `RO (2)`: Read-only access\\n  - `RW (3)`: Read-write access\\n- **Functions:**\\n  - `convertToAuthLevel()`: Parse auth level from VPack slice or string\\n  - `convertFromAuthLevel()`: Convert auth level to string\\n\\n## Authentication Flow Summary\\n\\n1. **Initial Authentication:** User sends credentials (basic auth or JWT) to `RestAuthHandler` via `/_open/auth`\\n2. **Token Validation:** `TokenCache::checkAuthentication()` validates the token using either:\\n   - Basic auth: Delegates to `UserManager::checkCredentials()`\\n   - JWT: Validates signature using stored secrets and checks expiry\\n3. **Authorization Context:** `ExecContext` is created with the authenticated user's permissions\\n4. **Request Processing:** Handler executes with context, using `ExecContext::current()` to check permissions\\n5. **User Management:** `RestUsersHandler` provides `/_api/user/` endpoint for user CRUD operations\\n6. **Persistence:** `UserManager` manages the `_system/_users` collection with caching and background sync\\n\\n## Key Security Features\\n\\n- **JWT Signature Algorithms:** Supports both HMAC-SHA256 and ES256 (ECDSA) for enterprise deployments\\n- **Secret Rotation:** Passive secrets allow JWT rotation without immediate server restart\\n- **Token Caching:** `TokenCache` with LRU cache reduces repeated authentication processing\\n- **Thread Safety:** `ReadWriteLock` protects concurrent access to user and token data\\n- **Permission Granularity:** Three-level permission model (database-level and collection-level)\\n- **Superuser Context:** Dedicated internal context for administrative operations\\n- **Session Timeouts:** Configurable session timeouts and JWT expiry constraints\"\n}\n",

JWT Token Validation\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/TokenCache.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `TokenCache`\\n- **Responsibility:** Caches and validates authentication tokens (both basic auth and JWT)\\n- **Key Methods:**\\n  - `checkAuthentication()`: Validates incoming auth tokens\\n  - `validateJwtBody()`: Parses and validates JWT token payload\\n  - `validateJwtHMAC256Signature()`: Validates HMAC-SHA256 JWT signatures\\n  - `validateJwtES256Signature()`: Validates ES256 (ECDSA) JWT signatures\\n- **Entry Structure:** Contains username, authentication status, expiry time, allowed paths, and roles\\n- **Features:**\\n  - Supports both HMAC-SHA256 and ES256 signature algorithms\\n  - Implements LRU cache for token entries\\n  - Manages both active and passive JWT secrets\\n\\n### 3. Authorization Context (Permission Checking)\\n**Location:** `arangod/Utils/ExecContext.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `ExecContext` (inherits from `RequestContext`)\\n- **Responsibility:** Maintains execution context with authorization information for each request\\n- **Key Features:**\\n  - Tracks current user, database, system-level auth level, and database-level auth level\\n  - Provides static `current()` method to access thread-local context\\n  - Implements superuser context via `ExecContext::Superuser` singleton\\n  - Methods:\\n    - `isSuperuser()`: Checks if user is superuser\\n    - `isAdminUser()`: Checks if user has admin privileges\\n    - `isInternal()`: Checks if context is internal operation\\n    - `isReadOnly()`: Checks if context is read-only\\n  - Uses scope guards: `ExecContextScope` and `ExecContextSuperuserScope`\\n\\n### 4. User Management REST API\\n**Location:** `arangod/RestHandler/RestUsersHandler.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `RestUsersHandler` (inherits from `RestBaseHandler`)\\n- **Responsibility:** Implements REST endpoint for user management\\n- **Endpoint:** `/_api/user/` (registered in `GeneralServerFeature`)\\n- **Supported Methods:**\\n  - `getRequest()`: List or retrieve user information\\n  - `postRequest()`: Create new user\\n  - `putRequest()`: Update user\\n  - `patchRequest()`: Partially update user\\n  - `deleteRequest()`: Delete user\\n- **Integration:** Uses `auth::UserManager` for persistence and `ExecContext` for authorization\\n\\n### 5. User Manager (User Data Management)\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/UserManager.h` (abstract interface) and `arangod/Auth/UserManagerImpl.h/cpp` (implementation)\\n- **Interface:** `UserManager` abstract base class\\n- **Implementation:** `UserManagerImpl` concrete class\\n- **Responsibility:** Central authority for user data, permissions, and caching\\n- **Key Features:**\\n  - Caches user data locally from `_system/_users` collection\\n  - Maintains background update thread for cache synchronization\\n  - Methods:\\n    - `storeUser()`: Create or replace user\\n    - `removeUser()`: Delete user\\n    - `updateUser()`: Update specific user\\n    - `accessUser()`: Read user without modification\\n    - `databaseAuthLevel()`: Check user's database permission\\n    - `collectionAuthLevel()`: Check user's collection permission\\n    - `checkCredentials()`: Validate username/password\\n    - `createAccessToken()`: Generate access tokens\\n    - `deleteAccessToken()`: Revoke access tokens\\n  - Thread-safe with read-write locks\\n\\n### 6. User Class\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/User.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `User`\\n- **Responsibility:** Represents a user object with permissions and metadata\\n- **Components:**\\n  - Username and password hash\\n  - Active/inactive status\\n  - Database-level permissions\\n  - Collection-level permissions\\n  - Extras (arbitrary metadata)\\n\\n### 7. Authentication Feature (Configuration)\\n**Location:** `arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationFeature.h` and `.cpp`\\n- **Class:** `AuthenticationFeature`\\n- **Responsibility:** Manages authentication system initialization and configuration\\n- **Key Responsibilities:**\\n  - Collects command-line options via `collectOptions()` (registered in startup)\\n  - Validates options via `validateOptions()`\\n  - Initializes `UserManager` and `TokenCache` in `prepare()`\\n  - Loads JWT secrets from file/folder\\n  - Provides singleton access via `instance()` static method\\n  - Methods:\\n    - `isActive()`: Check if authentication is enabled\\n    - `authenticationUnixSockets()`: Check Unix socket auth setting\\n    - `authenticationSystemOnly()`: Check if auth restricted to system database\\n    - `tokenCache()`: Access token cache instance\\n    - `userManager()`: Access user manager instance\\n    - `jwtSecrets()`: Retrieve JWT secrets for token validation\\n    - `loadJwtSecretsFromFile()`: Load secrets from disk\\n\\n### 8. Authentication Options (Default Settings)\\n**Location:** `arangod/GeneralServer/AuthenticationOptions.h`\\n- **Structure:** `AuthenticationOptions`\\n- **Default Values:**\\n  - `authenticationUnixSockets = true`: Allow Unix socket auth\\n  - `authenticationSystemOnly = true`: Restrict to system database\\n  - `active = true`: Authentication enabled by default\\n  - `sessionTimeout = 3600.0` seconds: 1 hour default session timeout\\n  - `minimalJwtExpiryTime = 10.0` seconds: Minimum JWT expiry\\n  - `maximalJwtExpiryTime = 3600.0` seconds: Maximum JWT expiry (1 hour)\\n  - `jwtSecretProgramOption`: Optional inline JWT secret\\n  - `jwtSecretKeyfileProgramOption`: Optional JWT secret keyfile path\\n  - `jwtSecretFolderProgramOption`: Optional JWT secrets folder path\\n\\n### 9. Auth Handler Interface\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/Handler.h`\\n- **Class:** `Handler` abstract interface\\n- **Responsibility:** Defines interface for pluggable authentication handlers\\n- **Methods:**\\n  - `authenticate()`: Authenticate user and return permissions\\n  - `readPermissions()`: Read user permissions for cached users\\n  - `refreshRate()`: Return cache refresh rate in seconds\\n  - `allowOfflineCacheUsage()`: Allow use of offline cache\\n\\n### 10. Common Auth Definitions\\n**Location:** `arangod/Auth/Common.h`\\n- **Enum:** `Level` defines authorization levels:\\n  - `UNDEFINED (0)`: No level defined\\n  - `NONE (1)`: No access\\n  - `RO (2)`: Read-only access\\n  - `RW (3)`: Read-write access\\n- **Functions:**\\n  - `convertToAuthLevel()`: Parse auth level from VPack slice or string\\n  - `convertFromAuthLevel()`: Convert auth level to string\\n\\n## Authentication Flow Summary\\n\\n1. **Initial Authentication:** User sends credentials (basic auth or JWT) to `RestAuthHandler` via `/_open/auth`\\n2. **Token Validation:** `TokenCache::checkAuthentication()` validates the token using either:\\n   - Basic auth: Delegates to `UserManager::checkCredentials()`\\n   - JWT: Validates signature using stored secrets and checks expiry\\n3. **Authorization Context:** `ExecContext` is created with the authenticated user's permissions\\n4. **Request Processing:** Handler executes with context, using `ExecContext::current()` to check permissions\\n5. **User Management:** `RestUsersHandler` provides `/_api/user/` endpoint for user CRUD operations\\n6. **Persistence:** `UserManager` manages the `_system/_users` collection with caching and background sync\\n\\n## Key Security Features\\n\\n- **JWT Signature Algorithms:** Supports both HMAC-SHA256 and ES256 (ECDSA) for enterprise deployments\\n- **Secret Rotation:** Passive secrets allow JWT rotation without immediate server restart\\n- **Token Caching:** `TokenCache` with LRU cache reduces repeated authentication processing\\n- **Thread Safety:** `ReadWriteLock` protects concurrent access to user and token data\\n- **Permission Granularity:** Three-level permission model (database-level and collection-level)\\n- **Superuser Context:** Dedicated internal context for administrative operations\\n- **Session Timeouts:** Configurable session timeouts and JWT expiry constraints\"\n}\n",
